# <a name="obsolete-types-in-the-net-framework"></a><span data-ttu-id="38b92-102">Tipos obsoletos no .NET Framework</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="38b92-102">Obsolete Types in the .NET Framework</span></span>

<a name="introduction"></a> <span data-ttu-id="38b92-103">As tabelas deste artigo listam os membros que estão obsoletos no .NET Framework 4.5 e 4.6, organizados por assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="38b92-103">The tables in this article list the types that are obsolete in the .NET Framework 4.5 and the .NET Framework 4.6, organized by assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="38b92-104">Use os links a seguir para ver uma lista dos tipos obsoletos e das alternativas recomendadas em cada assembly.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="38b92-104">Use the following links to see a list of the obsolete types and the recommended alternatives in each assembly.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="38b92-105">Como esses tipos são obsoletos, todos seus membros também estão obsoletos.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="38b92-105">Because these types are obsolete, all their members are also obsolete.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="38b92-106">Para obter uma lista de membros obsoletos adicionais na biblioteca de classes .NET Framework, confira [Membros obsoletos](obsolete-members.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="38b92-106">For a list of additional obsolete members in the .NET Framework class library, see [Obsolete Members](obsolete-members.md).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="38b92-134">As tabelas a seguir listam os tipos que foram declarados obsoletos em assemblies de sistema.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="38b92-134">The following tables list the types that have been declared obsolete in system assemblies.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="38b92-135">Esses assemblies são usados no desenvolvimento de aplicativos de uso\-geral direcionados ao .NET Framework.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="38b92-135">These assemblies are used for general\-purpose application development that targets the .NET Framework.</span></span>
